 is raily main bhi mamata banerjee ne centre kii modi sarkaar par jamkar nishaanaa saadhaa he

 Delhi Police Chief BS Bassi, in a very strong statement in the midst of his ongoing confrontation with the Arvind Kejriwal government, said today that if Delhi Police comes into the hands of the government of this city, it will be the 'most unfortunate' day in the history of the capital Delhi
 And she is doing a 'perfect' job under the center

 unhen (aap) ko ek raajnneetik maang karne kaa adhikaar he

 dilli ke ek naagarik ke taur par mujhe yah kehane kaa adhikaar he ki yah dilli ke nagarikon ke liye sahi nahin he

 Bassi said, 'the present system is the best
 kisi bhi pradhanmantri kaa dilli main koi nihit swaarth nahin, jab tak ki vah dilli ke naa hon
 i have not seen any prime minister in my career who has any local interest in Delhi
 ' He said, 'every Prime Minister wants the development of Delhi, but has no local vested interest

 He said, 'any reshuffle will be an injustice to the people of Delhi as this will not make the police strong but weaken them
 yadi aap pherbadal karte hai or use shahar kii sarkaar ke adheen kar dete hai to sthaneey nihit swaarth kaam karne lagenge
 i have worked in Goa, Pondicherry and on the basis of that i can say that if it is brought under the city government, local vested interests will start working
 ’ On the question of the AAP government considering to hold a referendum on the issue of full state, he said that this step would be 'unconstitutional'
 unhone kaha, ‘bhartiya samvidhan ke tahat koi bhi janamat sangrah asanvaidhanik he
 The present Indian Constitution does not allow any referendum and it will not be allowed unless there is an amendment in the Constitution
 yah asanvaidhanik krity hoga

 behatar hota anna or unki team is disha main or prayaas karti
 It helps people to decide who is capable of going to Parliament and Legislative Assemblies and who to stop from going
 ise dalgat raajnneeti se upar uthakar kiya ja saktaa tha
 His weapon of 'right to reject' was insistent on using it
 
 
 jo kamiyaan hai unhen dur karne kii ladaai bhi ladi ja sakati he
 Results would have come
 
 
 dhire-dhire aate, lekin jarur aate, log pehle se bhi kai dabaav samoohon ke prabhaav main vot karte aae hai
 Later he has also made changes
 anna ke andolan se, khaskar pehle charan se, kaaphi logon ne sikh lee
 
 
 He seemed more politically aware
 is charan ke baad kuch rajyon main hue chunaavon par uskaa saaf asar bhi dikhaa
 But now after jumping into politics, how much they will be able to do this work
 
 
 yah sochane laayak vishay he
 Corruption is an issue in Indian politics
 
 
 lekin sirf ek mudda hi he
 Apart from this, there are many other issues which affect politics
 vot daalane se pehle matadaata bhrashtachar ke saath-saath kai duusare masalon par bhi sochataa he or tab faisla karata he
 Anna will contest the election only on the issue of corruption and would like votes
 
 
 to unhen nahin milenge
 On issues like religion, caste, sub-caste and reservation, what attitude will Team Anna adopt and how will they make it in accordance with their nature, it will be a matter to be seen
 chante hue khantee raajnneetigyon ke saatha 'chausar kaa khel' khilne ke baad anna or unki team kaa chiraharan avashyambhavi lag rahaa he
 Who 'krishna' will save them from this rip-off
 
 
 yah bhi dekhne laayak hoga
 The comments kul milakar anna andolan khatm hota dikh rahaa he
 At this juncture, it can be said with certainty that the movement has gone astray
 balki andolan kii 'maut' ho chuki he
 It would have been better if Anna had given more political education to the people, and made them more ready to fight their own battles
 lekin, ek baat yah kahi ja sakati he ki desh kii yuva peedi ke ek hisse ko is andolan ke jariye yah bataane main anna andolan jarur safal hua ki kaise kisi masale par janamat jutaya jaae
 
 
 Especially when he is not able to get free time by bashing his head in Facebook and other gadgets
 
 
 
 Arvind Kejriwal has also told many ways how he will protect himself from 'kalima'
 kejariwal kaa kahana he ki unka uddeshy satta hathiyanna nahin he
 By ending the Delhi-centric government, they want to bring the government to more villages
 unke dal main koi bhi haikaman nahin hoga, ghoshnaa patr ko janata hi banaaegi
 
 
 And the special thing is that the parties whose leaders are feeling 'suffocated' in their party can join their 'patriot Movement'
 itnaa sab karne ke baad unke anusaar agle teen saalon main bharat 'badal' jayega
 This model of such a 'clean' and 'settled' approach is a completely new thing in recent politics
 lekin, ye ho saktaa he ki yah sambhav ho
 
 
 It may happen
 
 
 
 But there are many question marks on the intensity and potential of 'honest' efforts to achieve this ideal state
 netaaon kii maane to ek seat par chunaav ladane ke liye kam se kam 60 lakh rupayon kii jarurat padati he or isamen kaala dhan jodakar yah paanch-chah karod kaa aankada banataa he
 He has not made any specific disclosures about this 'necessary' money while contesting elections and where he will bring the 'force' to get it
 iske alaava sabase badi chunauti sabhi vidhansabhaon or sansad ke liye pratyaashiyon ke charitra kii 'guarantee' he
 Anna can take his guarantee, Kejriwal is also taking it
 
 
 lekin baakiyon kaa kya hoga
 There will be no doubt that they will be victims of scandalous politics
 aarope lagane ke baad kitne logon ko ve waapas lenge
 
 
 And how long they will wait to get a certificate of their clean character
 or sabase khaas baat
 
 
 How better and how soon they will be able to provide the option of those who will be accused
 in sawaalon ke jawaab yaa to team anna ne soche nahin hai yaa abhi tak bataae nahin hai
 They may have a 'formula' to deal with in the coming days, but so far it looks dark
 philhal ve chand un logon se esemes mangakar raajnneetik faisle kar rahe hai jo vot dene tak kii jahamat nahin uthaate hai
 60 per cent of the people who vote in every election do not even SMS
 tab phir kaise is ladaai ko jari rakhaa ja saktaa tha

 According to the leaders, to contest elections on one seat, at least 60 lakh rupees are required and by adding black money to it, it becomes a figure of five to six crores
 chunaav ladane ke dauraan yah 'jaruri' dhan or ise paane ke liye 'bal' vah kahaan se laaenge, iske bare main unhone koi khaas khulaasa nahin kiya he
 Apart from this, the biggest challenge is the 'guarantee' of the character of the candidates for all the assemblies and parliament
 anna apni guarantee le sakate hai, kejariwal bhi le rahe hai
 
 
 But what will happen to the rest
 chhichhaaledaar raajnneeti ke shikaar ve honge, isamen koi shaq nahin he
 How many people will they take back after being accused
 
 
 or kab tak unke saaf charitra hone kaa certificate praapt karne kaa intjaar karenge
 And the most special thing
 
 
 jin logon par aarope lagenge unka vikalp ve kitna behatar or kitni jaldi uplabdh kara paaenge
 The answers to these questions are either not thought by Team Anna or have not been told yet
 ho saktaa he aane vaale dinon main isse nipatane kaa koi 'formula' unke paas ho lekin abhi tak is par andhera hi dikhataa he
 Right now they are making political decisions by asking for SMS from those who do not even bother to vote
 har chunaav main vot daalane vaale 60 fisadi log to esemes karte hi nahin hai
 Then how could this fight continue? 
 
 kai tareeke the or hai
 
 
 But they need to be patient and keep ambitions out
 hamaare kareeb 60 saal puraane loktantr main ek raajnneetik ladaai or ek saamaajik ladaai ladane ke taur-tareeke alag-alag ho gaye hai
 Making social pressure on politics is easier and closer to possible
 raajnneetik partiyon par saamaajik dabaav banaakar chijen hasil kii ja sakati hai
 Anna and her team would have made more efforts in this direction
 yah tay karne main logon kii madad karti ki koun sansad or vidhansabhaon main jane ke kaabil he or kise jane se rokna he
 This could be done by rising above party politics
 'rhite tu riject' kaa unka hathiyaar tha, uskaa upyog karne par jor diya ja saktaa tha
 
 
 The battle to overcome the shortcomings can also be fought
 parinaam aate
 
 
 Slowly, but surely, people have already been voting under the influence of many pressure groups
 baad main unhone badlaav bhi kiye hai
 Many people learned from Anna's movement, especially from the first phase
 
 
 ve raajnneetik rup se zyada jaagruk lage
 It also showed a clear effect on the elections held in some states after this phase
 lekin ab raajnneeti main kudane ke baad ve is kaam ko kitna kar paaenge
 
 
 This is a topic worth thinking about
 bhartiya raajnneeti main bhrashtachar ek mudda he
 
 
 But there is only one issue
 iske alaava bhi kai or mudde hai jo raajnneeti ko prabhavit karte hai
 The voter thinks about corruption as well as many other issues before casting a vote and then decides
 anna sirf bhrashtachar ke masale par chunaav ladenge or vot bhi chahenge
 
 
 So they will not get it
 dharm, jati, upjati or aarakshan jaise masalon par team anna kya rukh apnayegi or ise kaise ve apni prakruti ke anuroop banaaenge, yah dekhne vaali baat hogi
 After playing 'chaucer's game' with the truncated politicians, Anna and his team seem unlikely
 koun 'krishna' unhen bachaayegaa is cheer haran se
 
 
 It will also be worth watching
 tippaniyan Overall, the Anna movement seems to be over
 is mode par, nishchit rup se kaha ja saktaa he ki andolan bhatak gaya he
 Rather, the movement has died
 behatar hota ki anna logon ko or zyada raajnneetik shiksha dete, unhen apni ladaai khud ladane ke liye or zyada taiyaar karte
 But, one thing can be said that the Anna movement definitely succeeded in telling a section of the younger generation of the country how to raise public opinion on some issue
